        <td id="L29" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="29"></td>

      <tr>
        <td id="L30" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="30"></td>
        <td id="LC30" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L31" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="31"></td>
        <td id="LC31" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\newpage</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L32" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="32"></td>
        <td id="LC32" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{Introduction}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{introduction}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L33" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="33"></td>
        <td id="LC33" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L34" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="34"></td>
        <td id="LC34" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Scientific claims should be subject to scrutiny by other researchers and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L35" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="35"></td>
        <td id="LC35" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the public at large. An important requirement for such scrutiny is that</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L36" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="36"></td>
        <td id="LC36" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">researchers make their claims transparent in a way that other</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L37" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="37"></td>
        <td id="LC37" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">researchers are able to use easily available resources to form a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L38" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="38"></td>
        <td id="LC38" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">complete understanding of the methods that were used by the original. In</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L39" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="39"></td>
        <td id="LC39" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the social sciences, especially given the personal computing and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L40" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="40"></td>
        <td id="LC40" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Internet revolutions and the wide availability of data and processing</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L41" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="41"></td>
        <td id="LC41" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">power, it is essential that data, code, and analyses be transparent.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L42" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="42"></td>
        <td id="LC42" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L43" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="43"></td>
        <td id="LC43" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This manual is intended to be a source mainly for empirical social</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L44" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="44"></td>
        <td id="LC44" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">science researchers who desire to make their own research transparent</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L45" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="45"></td>
        <td id="LC45" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to, and reproducible by, others. The entire process of research, from</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L46" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="46"></td>
        <td id="LC46" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">hypothesis generation to publication, is covered. Although norms differ</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L47" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="47"></td>
        <td id="LC47" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">across disciplines, we attempt to bring a broad view of the empirical</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L48" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="48"></td>
        <td id="LC48" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">social sciences to these recommendations, and hope that students and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L49" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="49"></td>
        <td id="LC49" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">researchers in any social science field may tailor these recommendations</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L50" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="50"></td>
        <td id="LC50" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to best fit their field.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L51" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="51"></td>
        <td id="LC51" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L52" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="52"></td>
        <td id="LC52" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The manual is laid out as follows: in section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{ethical-research} we first discuss the motivation for this document: the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L53" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="53"></td>
        <td id="LC53" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">desire to do ethical research. A major component of ethical social</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L54" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="54"></td>
        <td id="LC54" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">science research is treating research subjects appropriately. This is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L55" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="55"></td>
        <td id="LC55" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">mandated by federal law and overseen by Institutional Review Boards</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L56" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="56"></td>
        <td id="LC56" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(IRBs), and should be taken seriously by researchers. But just as</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L57" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="57"></td>
        <td id="LC57" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">treating subjects fairly is ethical, we believe that transparent,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L58" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="58"></td>
        <td id="LC58" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">reproducible research is also a major part of ethical research.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L59" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="59"></td>
        <td id="LC59" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L60" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="60"></td>
        <td id="LC60" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{study-design} we discuss study design, including how to power studies</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L61" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="61"></td>
        <td id="LC61" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">appropriately.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L62" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="62"></td>
        <td id="LC62" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L63" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="63"></td>
        <td id="LC63" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{registration} we discuss one of the major problems in non-transparent</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L64" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="64"></td>
        <td id="LC64" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">research, specifically publication bias. We also discuss how this</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L65" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="65"></td>
        <td id="LC65" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">problem can be resolved through the practice of registration.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L66" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="66"></td>
        <td id="LC66" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Publication bias stems from the fact that published results are</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L67" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="67"></td>
        <td id="LC67" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">overwhelmingly statistically significant. But without knowing how many</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L68" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="68"></td>
        <td id="LC68" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">tests were run (the number of unpublished results), it is impossible to know whether these significant</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L69" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="69"></td>
        <td id="LC69" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">results are meaningful, or whether they are the 5<span class="pl-cce">\%</span> of tests that we</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L70" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="70"></td>
        <td id="LC70" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">would expect to appear significant due to random sampling, even with no</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L71" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="71"></td>
        <td id="LC71" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">true effect. By publicly registering all studies, we can have a better</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L72" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="72"></td>
        <td id="LC72" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">idea of just how many tests have been run.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L73" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="73"></td>
        <td id="LC73" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L74" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="74"></td>
        <td id="LC74" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{rdof} we discuss researcher degrees of freedom and pre-analysis</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L75" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="75"></td>
        <td id="LC75" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">plans; In addition to registering trials, researchers can also</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L76" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="76"></td>
        <td id="LC76" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">specify their outcomes of interest and their exact methods of analysis</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L77" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="77"></td>
        <td id="LC77" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to bind their hands during the analysis phase by writing a Pre-Analysis</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L78" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="78"></td>
        <td id="LC78" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Plan (PAP). This is a relatively new idea in the social sciences, so</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L79" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="79"></td>
        <td id="LC79" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">there is not yet a consensus on when a PAP should be required, what the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L80" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="80"></td>
        <td id="LC80" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">ideal level of detail is, and how much it should constrain a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L81" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="81"></td>
        <td id="LC81" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">researcher&#39;s hands in the actual analysis, but by pre-specifying analyses,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L82" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="82"></td>
        <td id="LC82" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">researchers can distinguish between confirmatory and exploratory</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L83" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="83"></td>
        <td id="LC83" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">analysis. We do not necessarily place higher intrinsic value on one or</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L84" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="84"></td>
        <td id="LC84" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the other, but making the distinction clear is key for appropriate</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L85" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="85"></td>
        <td id="LC85" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">interpretation.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L86" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="86"></td>
        <td id="LC86" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L87" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="87"></td>
        <td id="LC87" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In section~<span class="pl-c1">\ref</span>{replication-and-reproducibility} we discuss workflow and materials sharing, with an eye on</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L88" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="88"></td>
        <td id="LC88" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">making research replicable by others. Researchers should make their code</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L89" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="89"></td>
        <td id="LC89" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and data publicly available so that others may repeat and verify their</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L90" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="90"></td>
        <td id="LC90" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">analysis. Making data available incentivizes researchers to make their</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L91" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="91"></td>
        <td id="LC91" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">work accurate in the first place, and makes replication easier for</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L92" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="92"></td>
        <td id="LC92" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">others, improving the scientific process, but also raises the concern of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L93" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="93"></td>
        <td id="LC93" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">differential privacy, since steps should be taken to prevent</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L94" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="94"></td>
        <td id="LC94" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">identification of individuals in the data. We also discuss the issue of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L95" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="95"></td>
        <td id="LC95" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">reporting standards: a standardized list of things that authors should</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L96" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="96"></td>
        <td id="LC96" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">report to help make their work reproducible.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>

      <tr>
        <td id="L188" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="188"></td>
        <td id="LC188" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>  The voluntary consent of the human subject is absolutely essential.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L189" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="189"></td>
        <td id="LC189" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L190" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="190"></td>
        <td id="LC190" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>  This means that the person involved should have legal capacity to give consent; should be so situated as to be able to exercise free power of choice, without the intervention of any element of force, fraud,  deceit, duress, over-reaching, or other ulterior form of constraint or coercion; and should have sufficient knowledge and comprehension of the elements of the subject matter involved as to enable him to make an understanding and enlightened decision. This latter element requires that before the acceptance of an affirmative decision by the experimental subject there should be made known to him the nature, duration, and purpose of the experiment; the method and means by which it is to be conducted; all inconveniences and hazards reasonably to be expected; and the effects upon his health or person which may possibly come from his participation in the experiment.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L191" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="191"></td>
        <td id="LC191" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L192" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="192"></td>
        <td id="LC192" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> The duty and responsibility for ascertaining the quality of the consent rests upon each individual who initiates, directs or engages in the experiment. It is a personal duty and responsibility which may not be delegated to another with impunity.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L193" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="193"></td>
        <td id="LC193" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\item</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L194" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="194"></td>
        <td id="LC194" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> The experiment should be such as to yield fruitful results for the good of society, unprocurable by other methods or means of study, and  not random and unnecessary in nature.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L195" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="195"></td>
        <td id="LC195" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\item</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L196" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="196"></td>
        <td id="LC196" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> The experiment should be so designed and based on the results of animal experimentation and a knowledge of the natural history of the disease or other problem under study that the anticipated results will  justify the performance of the experiment.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L197" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="197"></td>
        <td id="LC197" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\item</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L198" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="198"></td>
        <td id="LC198" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> The experiment should be so conducted as to avoid all unnecessary</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L199" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="199"></td>
        <td id="LC199" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>physical and mental suffering and injury.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L200" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="200"></td>
        <td id="LC200" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\item</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L201" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="201"></td>
        <td id="LC201" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> No experiment should be conducted where there is an a priori reason to believe that death or disabling injury will occur; except, perhaps, in  those experiments where the experimental physicians also serve as  subjects.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L202" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="202"></td>
        <td id="LC202" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\item</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L203" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="203"></td>
        <td id="LC203" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> The degree of risk to be taken should never exceed that determined by the humanitarian importance of the problem to be solved by the experiment.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L204" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="204"></td>
        <td id="LC204" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\item</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L205" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="205"></td>
        <td id="LC205" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> Proper preparations should be made and adequate facilities provided to protect the experimental subject against even remote possibilities of injury, disability, or death.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L206" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="206"></td>
        <td id="LC206" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\item</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L207" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="207"></td>
        <td id="LC207" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> The experiment should be conducted only by scientifically qualified persons. The highest degree of skill and care should be required through all stages of the experiment of those who conduct or engage in the experiment.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L208" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="208"></td>
        <td id="LC208" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\item</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L209" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="209"></td>
        <td id="LC209" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> During the course of the experiment the human subject should be at liberty to bring the experiment to an end if he has reached the  physical or mental state where continuation of the experiment seems to him to be impossible.</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L210" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="210"></td>
        <td id="LC210" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>\item</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L211" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="211"></td>
        <td id="LC211" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span> During the course of the experiment the scientist in charge must be prepared to terminate the experiment at any stage, if he has probably cause to believe, in the exercise of the good faith, superior skill and careful judgment required of him that a continuation of the experiment is likely to result in injury, disability, or death to the experimental subject.</span></td>
      </tr>

      </tr>

        <td id="LC267" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    Selection of Subjects: ``Individual justice in the selection of</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L268" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="268"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L271" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="271"></td>
        <td id="LC271" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    for risky research. Social justice requires that distinction be</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L272" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="272"></td>
        <td id="LC272" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    drawn between classes of subjects that ought, and ought not, to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L273" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="273"></td>
        <td id="LC273" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    participate in any particular kind of research, based on the ability</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L274" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="274"></td>
        <td id="LC274" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    of members of that class to bear burdens and on the appropriateness</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L275" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="275"></td>
        <td id="LC275" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">    of placing further burdens on already burdened persons.&quot;</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L276" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="276"></td>
        <td id="LC276" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  <span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{itemize}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L277" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="277"></td>

      </tr>

        <td id="L278" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="278"></td>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L279" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="279"></td>

      </tr>

      </tr>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L286" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="286"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L287" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="287"></td>
        <td id="LC287" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">five members, a mix of men and women, scientists and non-scientists, and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L288" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="288"></td>
        <td id="LC288" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">at least one member not affiliated with the institution. Since IRBs and</td>
      </tr>

        <td id="L289" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="289"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L290" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="290"></td>
        <td id="LC290" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">institution to institution, but one example can be seen at</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L291" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="291"></td>
        <td id="LC291" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{http://cphs.berkeley.edu}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L292" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="292"></td>
        <td id="LC292" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L293" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="293"></td>
        <td id="LC293" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When conducting research internationally, researchers should give their</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L294" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="294"></td>
        <td id="LC294" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">human subjects the same protections as those inside the US. Laws in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L295" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="295"></td>
        <td id="LC295" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">developing countries may not be as well-defined or enforced, but</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L296" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="296"></td>
        <td id="LC296" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">researchers should still register with their US institution&#39;s IRB, and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L297" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="297"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L298" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="298"></td>

      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L299" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="299"></td>
        <td id="LC299" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">from the <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{http://www.hhs.gov/ohrp/international/intlcompilation/2014intlcomp.pdf.pdf}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L300" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="300"></td>
        <td id="LC300" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">{Office for Human Research Protections}.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L301" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="301"></td>
        <td id="LC301" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L302" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="302"></td>
        <td id="LC302" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Another key resource for researchers and research conducted outside the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L303" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="303"></td>
        <td id="LC303" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">US is the <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{http://www.wma.net/en/30publications/10policies/b3/index.html}{Declaration of Helsinki} by the World Medical Association</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L304" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="304"></td>
        <td id="LC304" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(WMA). Originally adopted by the WMA in 1964, the document has significantly</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L305" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="305"></td>
        <td id="LC305" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">influenced the laws and regulations adopted to govern research</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L306" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="306"></td>
        <td id="LC306" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">worldwide.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L307" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="307"></td>
        <td id="LC307" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L308" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="308"></td>
        <td id="LC308" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Lest one think that ethical concerns are limited to monsters of bygone</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L309" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="309"></td>
        <td id="LC309" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">eras, we refer readers to a dilemma caused by a Montana state election experiment by</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L310" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="310"></td>
        <td id="LC310" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">researchers from <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{http://www.washingtonpost.com/blogs/monkey-cage/wp/2014/11/03/ethics-and-research-in-comparative-politics/}{Stanford and Dartmouth} in 2014, who sent 100,000 people official-looking election flyers bearing the state seal weeks before the election.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L311" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="311"></td>
        <td id="LC311" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L312" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="312"></td>
        <td id="LC312" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsubsection</span>{Training}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{training}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L313" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="313"></td>
        <td id="LC313" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L314" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="314"></td>
        <td id="LC314" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A large number of universities participate in the <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{https://www.citiprogram.org/}{Collaborative Institutional Training Initiative} at the University of Miami (CITI). Completing their course on Human</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L315" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="315"></td>
        <td id="LC315" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Subjects Research is often a requirement of being included on a research</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L316" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="316"></td>
        <td id="LC316" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">proposal. For anyone at an institution not affiliated with CITI, the NIH maintains an <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{https://phrp.nihtraining.com/users/login.php}{online training course} that is free and open to the public.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L317" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="317"></td>
        <td id="LC317" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L318" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="318"></td>
        <td id="LC318" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{Study Design}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{study-design}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L319" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="319"></td>
        <td id="LC319" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">There are many issues involving study design that are somewhat related to transparent research. For randomized trials, we refer readers to two excellent resources, <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{randomizationtoolkit} and <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{glennerster_running_2013}, which cover many aspects of how to design and implement an excellent field trial. For studies that are not necessarily randomized trials, we recommend <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{gertler_impact_2011} or <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{angrist2008mostly} for those with more statistics training. Here we briefly discuss one aspect of study design especially relevant for reproducible research: determining sample size through power calculations.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L320" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="320"></td>
        <td id="LC320" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L321" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="321"></td>
        <td id="LC321" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span>{Power Analysis}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{Conducting Power Analysis}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L322" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="322"></td>
        <td id="LC322" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>By CS</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L323" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="323"></td>
        <td id="LC323" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Given that researchers are working within a null hypothesis testing framework, the âpowerâ </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L324" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="324"></td>
        <td id="LC324" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">of a study, the probability of rejecting the null hypothesis when it is false, is extremely </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L325" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="325"></td>
        <td id="LC325" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">important. Though 80<span class="pl-cce">\%</span> power is held as a lower bound for acceptable power in many disciplines </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L326" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="326"></td>
        <td id="LC326" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">such as medical research, the actual power of studies can be much lower. For example, research </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L327" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="327"></td>
        <td id="LC327" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">by <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{button_power_2013} found that the median power in neuroscience was 21<span class="pl-cce">\%</span>. This means that </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L328" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="328"></td>
        <td id="LC328" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">if a study investigating a true effect were run 100 times, 79 studies would fail to reach significance, </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L329" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="329"></td>
        <td id="LC329" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">meaning that the chance of a false negative is extremely high. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L330" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="330"></td>
        <td id="LC330" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L331" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="331"></td>
        <td id="LC331" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Though false negatives are perhaps the most often discussed issue with low powered studies, they are not the only issue. A second issue is that low powered studies actually decrease the likelihood of a true positive <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{button_power_2013}. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L332" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="332"></td>
        <td id="LC332" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This means that when a low powered studies does find an effect, the lower the likelihood that this effect is true in </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L333" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="333"></td>
        <td id="LC333" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the population; it is relatively more likely that it is a false positive.  A third issue with low powered studies relates to effect </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L334" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="334"></td>
        <td id="LC334" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">sizes. Small, low powered studies that reach statistical significance will over-estimate the true effect size in the population <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{button_power_2013}. These inflated effect size estimates will make it difficult for others to properly power future </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L335" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="335"></td>
        <td id="LC335" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">studies, and the inaccuracy of the estimate may also be problematic for making decisions based on scientific results. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L336" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="336"></td>
        <td id="LC336" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L337" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="337"></td>
        <td id="LC337" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">An obvious way to help mitigate the problems of underpowered studies is to run studies with higher power. However, this </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L338" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="338"></td>
        <td id="LC338" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">process is not always that straightforward. As previously mentioned, effect sizes from published studies are often inflated, </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L339" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="339"></td>
        <td id="LC339" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and so may not provide the most accurate estimate. Meta-analyses can provide better information, but they also often suffer </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L340" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="340"></td>
        <td id="LC340" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">from publication bias and thus inflated effect sizes. Additionally, effect sizes may be highly heterogeneous between studies, </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L341" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="341"></td>
        <td id="LC341" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">even studies with the same materials and methodologies <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{many_labs}. Thus, using a single point estimate of an effect size </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L342" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="342"></td>
        <td id="LC342" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">from published literature may lead to inaccurate power calculations.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L343" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="343"></td>
        <td id="LC343" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L344" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="344"></td>
        <td id="LC344" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To combat these problems, alternatives to the standard power analysis have been suggested. For example, <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{perugini2014safeguard} </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L345" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="345"></td>
        <td id="LC345" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">have suggested a technique called `safeguard power&#39; which takes into account the uncertainty surrounding effect size estimates </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L346" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="346"></td>
        <td id="LC346" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">when conducting power analyses. Specifically, they suggest basing power calculations off of the effect size corresponding to the lower bound of a 60<span class="pl-cce">\%</span> confidence interval around the point estimate from published literature. Another approach by <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{mcshane_2014} takes into account the between study variation in effect sizes when conducting power analyses to give a more conservative estimate of the number of participants needed to reach a given level of statistical power. Yet another approach, which is also feasible when an effect size estimate from the previous literature is not available, is to determine the smallest effect size you wish to be able to detect, and power your study to find this effect size <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{bloom1995minimum}.  </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L347" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="347"></td>
        <td id="LC347" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L348" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="348"></td>
        <td id="LC348" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>GSC</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L349" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="349"></td>
        <td id="LC349" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Additionally, researchers may be able to help one another as well as decrease false-positives by publishing or clearly making available their power calculations. If a reader of a paper saw a clearly stated ``this trial was powered to detect an effect size of X,&#39;&#39; this would help to put the study into the appropriate statistical context. The parametric assumptions involved (such as the intra-cluster correlation) could also be publicly posted in study protocols to help other researchers learn reasonable assumptions for their own studies. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L350" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="350"></td>
        <td id="LC350" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span> {Practical Considerations}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L351" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="351"></td>
        <td id="LC351" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The impact of most of these calculations will in many cases mean a larger sample size than some disciplines are used to working with. There are several ways to mitigate the impact of this. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L352" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="352"></td>
        <td id="LC352" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L353" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="353"></td>
        <td id="LC353" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In psychology, a few of these possible solutions are presented in <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{openmaximizing}. Researchers can join crowd-sourced projects where multiple labs share protocols and produce the same experiment, as was done with 13 psychological effects and 36 samples and settings in <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{many_labs}. The <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{https://osf.io/wfc6u/}{Collaborative Replications and Education Project} (CREP) tracks findings that can be relatively easily replicated in a teaching setting. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L354" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="354"></td>
        <td id="LC354" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L355" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="355"></td>
        <td id="LC355" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Economists have also discusses how project budgets should play into study design, by maximizing power subject to a budget constraint <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{randomizationtoolkit}. When data collection is the main cost, the proportion of treatment and control should each be one half, but if treatment is expensive, power can be maximized subject to the project budget using the rule: ``the ratio of subjects in the treatment group to those in the comparison should be proportional to the inverse of the square root of their cots.&#39;&#39;  Another important contribution to this are of power maximization subject to a budget constraint is that power depends on the number of rounds of surveying, and also the autocorrelation of measurements over time. <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{mckenzie2012caseformoreT} shows that baseline data is of most power when autocorrelation is high, and repeated measurements post-treatment of most power when autocorrelation is low.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L356" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="356"></td>
        <td id="LC356" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L357" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="357"></td>
        <td id="LC357" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L358" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="358"></td>
        <td id="LC358" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L359" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="359"></td>
        <td id="LC359" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L360" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="360"></td>
        <td id="LC360" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L361" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="361"></td>
        <td id="LC361" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">%</span>%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%</span></td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L362" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="362"></td>
        <td id="LC362" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\section</span>{Registration}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{registration}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L363" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="363"></td>
        <td id="LC363" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L364" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="364"></td>
        <td id="LC364" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">One of the problems brought into focus recently is publication bias.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L365" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="365"></td>
        <td id="LC365" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Publication bias is the selective publication of only significant</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L366" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="366"></td>
        <td id="LC366" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">results. Thankfully, there are tools available for researchers to combat</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L367" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="367"></td>
        <td id="LC367" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">these problems.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L368" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="368"></td>
        <td id="LC368" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L369" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="369"></td>
        <td id="LC369" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span>{Publication Bias}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{publication-bias}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L370" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="370"></td>
        <td id="LC370" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L371" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="371"></td>
        <td id="LC371" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">One of the primary drivers of the recent move towards transparency is</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L372" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="372"></td>
        <td id="LC372" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">increased awareness of publication bias. Numerous papers use collections</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L373" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="373"></td>
        <td id="LC373" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">of published papers to show that the proportion of significant results</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L374" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="374"></td>
        <td id="LC374" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">are extremely unlikely to come from any true population distribution</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L375" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="375"></td>
        <td id="LC375" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{delong_are_1992, gerber_testing_2001,  ioannidis_why_2005}. By examining the publication rates of null results and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L376" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="376"></td>
        <td id="LC376" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">significant results from a large set of NSF-funded studies, <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{franco_publication_2014} show that the selective publication of only</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L377" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="377"></td>
        <td id="LC377" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">significant results may stem from the fact that social science</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L378" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="378"></td>
        <td id="LC378" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">researchers largely fail to write up and submit results from studies</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L379" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="379"></td>
        <td id="LC379" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">resulting in null findings, citing lack of interest or fear of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L380" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="380"></td>
        <td id="LC380" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">rejection. This idea of rejecting, or not even submitting for review, papers with null-results, is commonly referred to as the ``file drawer problem&#39;&#39; <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{rosenthal1979file}. In fact, the percentage of null findings published in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L381" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="381"></td>
        <td id="LC381" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">journals appears to have been decreasing over time, across all</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L382" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="382"></td>
        <td id="LC382" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">disciplines <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{fanelli_negative_2012}. It seems unlikely that this would</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L383" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="383"></td>
        <td id="LC383" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">be an accurate reflection of the state of the universe, unless the hypotheses that scientists are testing are systematically changing over time. If journals only</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L384" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="384"></td>
        <td id="LC384" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">publish statistically significant results, we have no idea how many of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L385" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="385"></td>
        <td id="LC385" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">those significant results are evidence of real effects, and which are</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L386" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="386"></td>
        <td id="LC386" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the 5<span class="pl-cce">\%</span> of random draws that we should expect to show a significant</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L387" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="387"></td>
        <td id="LC387" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">result with a true zero effect. One way to combat this problem is to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L388" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="388"></td>
        <td id="LC388" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">require registration of all studies undertaken. Ideally we then search</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L389" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="389"></td>
        <td id="LC389" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the registry for studies of X on Y. If numerous studies show an</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L390" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="390"></td>
        <td id="LC390" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">effect, we have confidence the effect is real. If 5<span class="pl-cce">\%</span> of studies show a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L391" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="391"></td>
        <td id="LC391" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">significant effect, we give these outlier studies less credence.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L392" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="392"></td>
        <td id="LC392" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L393" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="393"></td>
        <td id="LC393" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\subsection</span>{Trial Registration}<span class="pl-c1">\label</span>{trial-registration}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L394" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="394"></td>
        <td id="LC394" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L395" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="395"></td>
        <td id="LC395" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A basic definition of registration is to publicly declare <span class="pl-c1">\emph</span>{all}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L396" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="396"></td>
        <td id="LC396" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">research that one plans on conducting. Ideally this is done in a public</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L397" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="397"></td>
        <td id="LC397" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">registry designed to accept registrations in the given research discipline,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L398" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="398"></td>
        <td id="LC398" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">and ideally the registration takes place before data collection begins.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L399" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="399"></td>
        <td id="LC399" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L400" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="400"></td>
        <td id="LC400" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Registration of randomized trials has achieved wide adoption in medicine, but is still</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L401" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="401"></td>
        <td id="LC401" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">relatively new to the social sciences. After congress passed a law in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L402" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="402"></td>
        <td id="LC402" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">1997 requiring the creation of a registry for FDA-regulated trials, and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L403" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="403"></td>
        <td id="LC403" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">the NIH created clinicaltrials.gov in 2000, The International Committee</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L404" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="404"></td>
        <td id="LC404" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">of Medical Journal Editors (ICMJE), a collection of editors of top</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L405" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="405"></td>
        <td id="LC405" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">medical journals, instituted a policy of publishing only registered</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L406" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="406"></td>
        <td id="LC406" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">trials in 2005 <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{DeAngelis2004}, and the policy has spread to</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L407" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="407"></td>
        <td id="LC407" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">other journals and been generally accepted by researchers <span class="pl-c1">\citep</span>{laine_clinical_2007}. Several other countries have their own national trial registries, and the World Health Organization created the <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{http://www.who.int/ictrp/about/en/}{International Clinical Trials Registry Platform (ICTRP)} in 2007 to automatically collect all this information in one place.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L408" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="408"></td>
        <td id="LC408" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L409" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="409"></td>
        <td id="LC409" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A profound example of the benefit of trial registries is detailed in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L410" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="410"></td>
        <td id="LC410" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{turner_selective_2008}, which details the publication rates of studies</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L411" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="411"></td>
        <td id="LC411" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">related to FDA-approved antidepressants. (See also <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{ioannidis_effectiveness_2008}.)</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L412" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="412"></td>
        <td id="LC412" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The outcome is perhaps what the most hardened cynic would expect:</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L413" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="413"></td>
        <td id="LC413" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">essentially all the trials with positive outcomes were published, a</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L414" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="414"></td>
        <td id="LC414" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">50/50 mix of questionable-outcome studies were published, and a majority of the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L415" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="415"></td>
        <td id="LC415" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">negative-outcome studies were unpublished a minimum of four years after the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L416" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="416"></td>
        <td id="LC416" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">study was completed. The figure below shows the drastically different</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L417" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="417"></td>
        <td id="LC417" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">rates of publication, and a large amount of publication bias.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L418" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="418"></td>
        <td id="LC418" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\begin</span>{center}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L419" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="419"></td>
        <td id="LC419" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\includegraphics</span>{TurnerFigure1.PNG}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L420" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="420"></td>
        <td id="LC420" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L421" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="421"></td>
        <td id="LC421" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Panel A of Figure 1 from <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{turner_selective_2008}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L422" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="422"></td>
        <td id="LC422" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"><span class="pl-c1">\end</span>{center}</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L423" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="423"></td>
        <td id="LC423" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Of course for this sort of exercise to be possible, unless a reader</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L424" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="424"></td>
        <td id="LC424" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">merely assumes that a registered trial without an associated published</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L425" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="425"></td>
        <td id="LC425" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">paper produced a null result (as in <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{rosenthal1979file}), it requires that the registration site</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L426" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="426"></td>
        <td id="LC426" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">itself obtain outcomes of trials. <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{http://www.clinicaltrials.gov}{ClinicalTrials.gov} is the only</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L427" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="427"></td>
        <td id="LC427" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">publicly available trial registry that requires such reporting of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L428" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="428"></td>
        <td id="LC428" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">results, and only for certain FDA trials.<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{<span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{resultscompliance} finds that compliance with results reporting even among those required was fairly low (22<span class="pl-cce">\%</span>). HHS and NIH took steps in November 2014 to expand the amount of results reporting required. See <span class="pl-c1">\url</span>{http://www.nih.gov/news/health/nov2014/od-19.htm}}  <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{hartung_reporting_2014} raises</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L429" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="429"></td>
        <td id="LC429" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">concerns about discrepancies between reporting of outcomes in published</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L430" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="430"></td>
        <td id="LC430" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">papers and in the <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{http://www.clinicaltrials.gov}{ClinicalTrials.gov} database; as many as 20<span class="pl-cce">\%</span> of</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L431" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="431"></td>
        <td id="LC431" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">studies had discrepancies in primary outcomes and as many as 33<span class="pl-cce">\%</span> had</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L432" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="432"></td>
        <td id="LC432" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">discrepancies in reporting of adverse events, so there is definitely room for improvement. </td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L433" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="433"></td>
        <td id="LC433" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L434" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="434"></td>
        <td id="LC434" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Even with dramatic growth in medical trial registration, problems</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L435" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="435"></td>
        <td id="LC435" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">remain. Not all journals have adopted the ICMJE policy, and complete</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L436" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="436"></td>
        <td id="LC436" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">enforcement is elusive. <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{mathieu_s_comparison_2009} looked at trials related</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L437" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="437"></td>
        <td id="LC437" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">to three medical conditions and found that only 46<span class="pl-cce">\%</span> of studies were</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L438" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="438"></td>
        <td id="LC438" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">registered before the end of the trial with primary outcomes clearly</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L439" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="439"></td>
        <td id="LC439" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">specified. Even among those adequately registered, 31<span class="pl-cce">\%</span> showed some</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L440" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="440"></td>
        <td id="LC440" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">discrepancies between registered and published outcomes, with bias in</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L441" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="441"></td>
        <td id="LC441" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">favor of statistically significant definitions.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L442" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="442"></td>
        <td id="LC442" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L443" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="443"></td>
        <td id="LC443" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Almost all registration efforts have thus far been limited to randomized</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L444" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="444"></td>
        <td id="LC444" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">control trials, as opposed to observational data. We believe</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L445" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="445"></td>
        <td id="LC445" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">that registering all types of analysis should be accepted and encouraged, though there are definitely concerns to registering observational work---not least of which is the inability to verify that registration preceded analysis. See <span class="pl-c1">\cite</span>{dal-re_making_2014} for a recent discussion of the pros and cons.</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L446" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="446"></td>
        <td id="LC446" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line"> </td>
      </tr>

      </tr>

        <td id="L477" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="477"></td>

</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L478" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="478"></td>
        <td id="LC478" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In political science, <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{http://e-gap.org/design-registration}{EGAP: Experiments in Governance and Politics} has</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L479" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="479"></td>
        <td id="LC479" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">created a registry as ``an unsupervised stopgap function to store</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L480" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="480"></td>
        <td id="LC480" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">designs until the creation of a general registry for social science</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L481" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="481"></td>
        <td id="LC481" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">research. The EGAP registry focuses on designs for experiments and</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L482" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="482"></td>
        <td id="LC482" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">observational studies in governance and politics.&#39;&#39; EGAP&#39;s registry had 93</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L483" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="483"></td>
        <td id="LC483" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">designs registered as of October 2014.<span class="pl-c1">\footnote</span>{Earlier less-widely</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L484" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="484"></td>
        <td id="LC484" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  adopted attempts to create registries in political science are the</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L485" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="485"></td>
        <td id="LC485" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  Political Science Registered Studies Dataverse (PSRSD,</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L486" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="486"></td>
        <td id="LC486" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  <span class="pl-c1">\href</span>{../customXml/item1.xml}{http://spia.uga.edu/faculty<span class="pl-cce">\_</span>pages/monogan/registration.php})</td>
      </tr>
      <tr>
        <td id="L487" class="blob-num js-line-number" data-line-number="487"></td>
